< text>
Do not buy with Tuff Shed! You are better buying from any other Shed place! I purchased a lovely shed that they had displayed outside. I waited for the shed to go into production and to be delivered. I understand that cause of Covid-19 it is backed up on delivery I don't have a problem with that its fine, but however I do have a problem with the way I received my shed! Damaged and bent material and used material! I did not want to accept it but the installers told me that they are just installers not the fabricators and this is what they have that I need to contact the manufacturer. I said ok but I don't want that damaged used shed and they said if they take it back I will have to pay 15% of the price! In short they are telling me that I'm forced to take the broken used shed or else I will have to pay for their broken used shed! They installed it and they did absolutely their best in trying to make it work but however even with their best they cannot fix the manufacturer defects. The shed has nail holes all over it, because it has been used before and disassembled then sent to me. It has cracks and many other defects. The roof is basically holding on a nail! I contacted customer service and was sent to Warranty manager John and it looks like he is the only guy that actually answers the phone, but however he claims that because of Covid-19 they are using any wood they have left in storage. In short used material. He said they will fix the holes with silicone. That is absolutely horrible because with in a year or less that silicone will form mold. I have that experience with where I live. I contacted the seller Tom and showed him the status of my shed and even he was shocked. He said he was going to send all the pictures and everything to the main manager of Tuff Shed and the only person that is actually trying to do anything is John, the so called main manager basically tuck his tail between his legs and disappeared from this earth because I was supposed to get a call within 24 hours..weeks passed and I didn't get anything. I'm stuck with a USED shed that was sold to me for NEW price. Absolutely horrible quality and material. Unsafe and a big safety hazard. It is like buying a new car and receiving the car with dents and being told that if you don't take it they will charge 15% of the price and when you are forced to take it they tell you they will take it to the shop and pull the dents out. Doesn't make it new, but I'm guessing NEW and USED is the same word to Tuff Shed. Everyone please stay away from this company! They scam, lie, hustle, and their people in power ignore. Save your money and you are better with any other shed company, even a handyman will do a better job than their 2year old that fabricates their wood. They do not stand by their word on quality at all! Have a look at my pictures. If you want a shed like mine with those problems, then by all means go buy Tuff Shed. Pictures speak louder than words. I was going to buy bigger sheds into a house size with Tuff Shed but after this NEVER AGAIN! I don't recommend to anyone to use this company! A file has been claimed to the Better Business Bureau, hopefully they can resolve and report this company. Thank you all for taking the time to read this. Stay away from Tuff Shed and stay safe! God Bless.</text>

(This finally got fixed by my original sales guy, but...)

< Review>
Ben gave me my favorite haircut I've ever had.

I don't think I have found one person until now that can cut my hair the way I want. I showed him a picture of a blade used to cut hair, and I asked him if he used something like that.  I recently found out about this type of tool used to cut hair.  Most of the time I try a new barber, the first thing they would say is that my hair is so thick.  Then they would use cutting shears like crazy to try to thin it out.  I told Ben about this, and he gets me completely.  He explained to me that they do this to try to fix the mistake they did to my hair, and it just makes it worse.

Ben was very confident cutting my hair, and he even mentioned that my hair had a "feather" look to it from the back.  He listens to what you want and don't want, and tries to  give you the exact haircut you want the way you want.

< Text>
I write a fair amount of reviews but this one is a bit more special.. I went out to Palm Springs to spend a few days with my mom. We were eating breakfast and I noticed she was sitting a bit odd. When I asked about why, she mentioned that her upper and lower back were sore..  I immediately checked the date on her mattress and it was very old. So right after breakfast I took her to buy a new mattress...  I thought for sure that it was going to be many hours and many mattress stores to find the right one for her... Thank God we went into Mattress Firm. We were greeted warmly by Ron, and I don't think I have ever encountered a more enthusiastic, genuine and patient sales associate IN MY LIFE.. My mom, at 89, is not the easiest person to deal with, she labors forever just to pick out crackers for a dinner party, so I knew that picking out a new mattress would require a sales associate with special skill... Ron spent over an hour with her and was lazer focussed as my mom detailed all her requirements. I have to tell you that I was amazed at Ron's ability, truly amazed...  He spent an hour and a 1/2 with her  Trying bed after bed. When they were done Ron had sound her just the right mattress. She has had it several weeks now and her back pain is completely gone and she gleefully talks about getting a great night sleep every night...  If you are on the lookout for a new mattress I can emphatically tell you you're not going to find any better place with any better sales associate. Ask Ron to help you and you'll be amazed< /Text>

< Review>
I ordered this spot as delivery a while back and thought it was exceptional. Made a promise to myself I'd go visit it in the flesh. Well, it wasn't so good live. Also, quite overpriced. You can get all these dishes for a tastier fare in NoHo. But hey, I live in this area so authentic asian isn't exactly available so this comes kinda close so I understand the price bump. My chicken over rice was a HUGE disappointment. The chicken should be tender and not dry. Shouldn't taste like trader joe's "just chicken". The duck rice at $16 was ridiculous. They must know what a rip off and how far they veered off from the tradition of duck rice. I'm really sad about that. Wonton soup was ok. very basic, Slightly over salty. Coconut ice cream, I didn't like at first but the more I ate it the more addicted I got. Very icy, but refreshing. Chicken wings, and I love chicken wings... I had one and was over.

Meh - if i come here again I'd just go for basic Thai dishes because all the authentic stuff they fake out and don't really hit that LEGIT mark.</Review>

If you're in the mood for the best Thai food then this is your place!
Lucky for me this restaurant is less than 5 minutes from my house. It's usually the busiest around lunch time since they have happy hour deals as well. But I came here around 7pm for dinner. The place is under new management and they have cleaned up very nicely and the staff is very friendly.
Right off the bat I ordered a Thai tea milk drink with boba added. They brought that out very quickly and it was so so delicious!! The boba was fresh and soft
Next I decided to get the coconut shrimp soup which is called Tom Kah Goong Shrimp Soup, the Exotic Thai Fried Rice and Pad See Ew which is cooked with wide flat rice noddle. All three entrees came out together and they all looked incredible. I started with the Tom Kah Goong. It had a small flame underneath to keep the soup warm. It was so delicious!! My god that ginger taste and the shrimp cooked perfectly and it was coconuty. It was out of this world good. Next, the fried rice was cooked deliciously. The small Chinese sausage inside gave a nice texture and flavor. Loved it! Lastly, the Pad See Ew was also delicious. The peanut sauce and the veggies were perfectly cooked together and created a very delicious aroma.
Over all I loved it here. I now know what the hype is all about. We will be ordering from them a lot more now.
P.S. they do a lot of take out orders which is a huge plus</review>

OMG DELICIOUS! My new go to spot for Thai food in Burbank.

If you love Thai food don't let this place go on untried. The wife had the spicy eggplant with beef and I ordered the spicy Penang curry with chicken.

Got to say the flavor was amazing, can't say enough good things about how delicious it was. I was surprised it was so good and I can't wait to come back and try more dishes.

Not a lot of people enjoying this fabulous restaurant so our service was immediate. We ordered from the lunch special menu. Lunch special prices are $10 a plate. It comes with salad and egg roll white or brown rice. The rice is shaped like a heart which was a cute touch.

They have a happy hour from 4:00 to 7:00 with $3 beers. Designated parking in front street parking around the side.</text>
